(1)(c / criticize-01

          :mod (m / military)
          :poss (c2 / country
                  :name (n / name
                          :op1 "Russia")))
  :ARG1 (c3 / company

                  :op1 "Kamchatenergo"
                  :op2 "Power"
                  :op3 "Company"))
  :ARG2 (i / impose-01
          :ARG0 c3
          :ARG1 (s / shutdown)
          :ARG2 (s2 / supply-01
                  :ARG2 (c4 / center
                          :ARG0-of (c5 / command-02)
                          :ARG0-of (g / guide-01
                                     :ARG1 (s3 / satellite
                                             :mod m
                                             :location (o / orbit)))
                          :ARG0-of (c6 / contribute-01
                                     :ARG2 (s4 / system
                                             :ARG0-of (c7 / control-01
                                                        :ARG1 (s5 / station
                                                                :mod (i2 / international)
                                                                :location (s6 / space)))))))))

(2)(a / authority
          :mod (m / military)
          :poss (c2 / country
                  :name (n / name
                          :op1 "Russia")))

(3)(i / impose-01
          :ARG0 c3
          :ARG1 (s / shutdown)
          :ARG2 (s2 / supply-01
                  :ARG2 (c4 / center
                          :ARG0-of (c5 / command-02)
                          :ARG0-of (g / guide-01
                                     :ARG1 (s3 / satellite
                                             :mod m
                                             :location (o / orbit)))
